    Purpose     : Random mix read/write 70/30 has abnormal performance drop.

                  modify other associated timer.

﻿Date: 2021/04/19
1.  Modification: To prevent GC speed is too slow if in GC EMGR and LOCK mode
    Purpose     : In update FW with heavy IO, IO will stop when update FW and thus GC will slow down, but after FW update, host write is heavy 
                  and free blocks will be slowly decreased, finally enter read_only_mode if GC speed is too low
    Root cause  : Corner case of GC speed control    
    BID         : RD daily life  
    Files       : [rdisk.c][ftl_core_gc.c][gc.c]
    Functions   : see shr_gc_no_slow_down
    Modifier    : Adams Chuang

2.  Modification: Clear GC flow control flag should sync with GC Mode, not only refert to free blocks
    Purpose     : Flag is set in ftl_core_gc_start, any GC behavior will enter gc_start (LOCK/EMGR/FORCE/SHUTTLE/WL/RD/DR),
                  if flag is nor properly cleared after GC, BTN timeout and evt by cpu4 panic occurs when host write
    Root cause  : Flag is cleared only in GC end by free block counts, there are other cases cause the flag not cleared    
    BID         : Jira 242 (POR free blk return to 25) / Jira 177 (shuttle GC set flag but free blk < 24, do not clear flag)
    Files       : [ftl_core_gc.c][gc.c]
    Functions   : see shr_gc_fc_ctrl and GC_Mode_DeAssert()
    Modifier    : Adams Chuang﻿
